    23	
    24	import java.nio.file.Path;
    25	import java.util.ArrayList;
    26	import java.util.List;
    27	import java.util.function.BiFunction;
    28	import java.util.regex.Pattern;
    29	
    30	import static com.microsoft.playwright.impl.LocatorUtils.*;
    31	import static com.microsoft.playwright.impl.Serialization.gson;
    32	import static com.microsoft.playwright.impl.Utils.convertType;
    33	
    34	class LocatorImpl implements Locator {
    35	  final FrameImpl frame;
    36	  final String selector;
    37	
    38	  LocatorImpl(FrameImpl frame, String selector, LocatorOptions options) {
    39	    this(frame, selector, options, null);
    40	  }
    41	
    42	  private LocatorImpl(FrameImpl frame, String selector, LocatorOptions options, Boolean visible) {
    43	    this.frame = frame;
    44	    if (options != null) {
    45	      if (options.hasText != null) {
    46	        selector += " >> internal:has-text=" + escapeForTextSelector(options.hasText, false);
    47	      }
    48	      if (options.hasNotText != null) {
    49	        selector += " >> internal:has-not-text=" + escapeForTextSelector(options.hasNotText, false);
    50	      }
    51	      if (options.has != null) {
    52	        LocatorImpl locator = (LocatorImpl) options.has;
    53	        if (locator.frame != frame)
    54	          throw new Error("Inner 'has' locator must belong to the same frame.");
    55	        selector += " >> internal:has=" + gson().toJson(locator.selector);
    56	      }
    57	      if (options.hasNot != null) {
    58	        LocatorImpl locator = (LocatorImpl) options.hasNot;
    59	        if (locator.frame != frame)
    60	          throw new Error("Inner 'hasNot' locator must belong to the same frame.");
    61	        selector += " >> internal:has-not=" + gson().toJson(locator.selector);
    62	      }
    63	    }
    64	    if (visible != null) {
    65	      selector += " >> visible=" + visible;
    66	    }
    67	    this.selector = selector;
    68	  }
    69	
    70	  private <R, O> R withElement(BiFunction<ElementHandle, O, R> callback, O options, String title) {
    71	    return frame.withTitle(title, () -> {
    72	      ElementHandleOptions handleOptions = convertType(options, ElementHandleOptions.class);
    73	      // TODO: support deadline based timeout
    74	      //    Double timeout = null;
    75	      //    if (handleOptions != null) {
    76	      //      timeout = handleOptions.timeout;
    77	      //    }
    78	      //    timeout = frame.page.timeoutSettings.timeout(timeout);
    79	      //    long deadline = System.nanoTime() + (long) timeout.doubleValue() * 1_000_000;
    80	      ElementHandle handle = elementHandle(handleOptions);
    81	      try {
    82	        return callback.apply(handle, options);
    83	      } finally {
    84	        if (handle != null) {
    85	          handle.dispose();
    86	        }
    87	      }
    88	    });
    89	  }
    90	
    91	  @Override
    92	  public List<Locator> all() {
    93	    List<Locator> result = new ArrayList<>();
    94	    int count = this.count();
    95	    for (int i = 0; i < count; i++) {
    96	      result.add(nth(i));
    97	    }

    51	  FrameImpl(ChannelOwner parent, String type, String guid, JsonObject initializer) {
    52	    super(parent, type, guid, initializer);
    53	
    54	    name = initializer.get("name").getAsString();
    55	    url = initializer.get("url").getAsString();
    56	    if (initializer.has("parentFrame")) {
    57	      parentFrame = connection.getExistingObject(initializer.getAsJsonObject("parentFrame").get("guid").getAsString());
    58	      parentFrame.childFrames.add(this);
    59	    }
    60	    for (JsonElement item : initializer.get("loadStates").getAsJsonArray()) {
    61	      loadStates.add(loadStateFromProtocol(item.getAsString()));
    62	    }
    63	  }
    64	
    65	  private static WaitUntilState loadStateFromProtocol(String value) {
    66	    switch (value) {
    67	      case "load": return LOAD;
    68	      case "domcontentloaded": return DOMCONTENTLOADED;
    69	      case "networkidle": return NETWORKIDLE;
    70	      case "commit": return COMMIT;
    71	      default: throw new PlaywrightException("Unexpected value: " + value);
    72	    }
    73	  }
    74	
    75	  @Override
    76	  public ElementHandle querySelector(String selector, QuerySelectorOptions options) {
    77	    if (options == null) {
    78	      options = new QuerySelectorOptions();
    79	    }
    80	    JsonObject params = gson().toJsonTree(options).getAsJsonObject();
    81	    params.addProperty("selector", selector);
    82	    JsonElement json = sendMessage("querySelector", params, NO_TIMEOUT);
    83	    JsonObject element = json.getAsJsonObject().getAsJsonObject("element");
    84	    if (element == null) {
    85	      return null;
    86	    }
    87	    return connection.getExistingObject(element.get("guid").getAsString());
    88	  }

   113	    LocatorImpl other = (LocatorImpl) locator;

   115	      throw new Error("Locators must belong to the same frame.");

    17	package com.microsoft.playwright.impl;
    18	
    19	import com.microsoft.playwright.Locator;
    20	import com.microsoft.playwright.options.AriaRole;
    21	
    22	import java.util.regex.Pattern;
    23	
    24	import static com.microsoft.playwright.impl.Serialization.gson;
    25	import static com.microsoft.playwright.impl.Utils.toJsRegexFlags;
    26	
    27	public class LocatorUtils {
    28	  static String getByTextSelector(Object text, Locator.GetByTextOptions options) {
    29	    boolean exact = options != null && options.exact != null && options.exact;
    30	    return "internal:text=" + escapeForTextSelector(text, exact);
    31	  }
    32	
    33	  static String getByLabelSelector(Object text, Locator.GetByLabelOptions options) {
    34	    boolean exact = options != null && options.exact != null && options.exact;
    35	    return "internal:label=" + escapeForTextSelector(text, exact);
    36	  }
    37	
    38	  private static String getByAttributeTextSelector(String attrName, Object value, boolean exact) {
    39	    return "internal:attr=[" + attrName + "=" + escapeForAttributeSelector(value, exact) + "]";
    40	  }
    41	
    42	  static String describeSelector(String description) {
    43	    return "internal:describe=" + gson().toJson(description);
    44	  }
    45	
    46	  static String getByTestIdSelector(Object testId, PlaywrightImpl playwright) {
    47	    return getByAttributeTextSelector(playwright.selectors.testIdAttributeName, testId, true);
    48	  }
    49	
    50	  static String getByAltTextSelector(Object text, Locator.GetByAltTextOptions options) {
    51	    boolean exact = options != null && options.exact != null && options.exact;
    52	    return getByAttributeTextSelector("alt", text, exact);
    53	  }
    54	
    55	  static String getByTitleSelector(Object text, Locator.GetByTitleOptions options) {
    56	    boolean exact = options != null && options.exact != null && options.exact;
    57	    return getByAttributeTextSelector("title", text, exact);
    58	  }
    59	
    60	  static String getByPlaceholderSelector(Object text, Locator.GetByPlaceholderOptions options) {
    61	    boolean exact = options != null && options.exact != null && options.exact;
    62	    return getByAttributeTextSelector("placeholder", text, exact);
    63	  }
    64	
    65	  private static void addAttr(StringBuilder result, String name, String value) {
    66	    result.append("[").append(name).append("=").append(value).append("]");
    67	  }
    68	
    69	  static String getByRoleSelector(AriaRole role, Locator.GetByRoleOptions options) {
    70	    StringBuilder result = new StringBuilder();
    71	    result.append("internal:role=").append(role.name().toLowerCase());
    72	    if (options != null) {
    73	      if (options.checked != null)
    74	        addAttr(result, "checked", options.checked.toString());
    75	      if (options.disabled != null)
    76	        addAttr(result, "disabled", options.disabled.toString());
    77	      if (options.selected != null)
    78	        addAttr(result, "selected", options.selected.toString());
    79	      if (options.expanded != null)
    80	        addAttr(result, "expanded", options.expanded.toString());
    81	      if (options.includeHidden != null)
    82	        addAttr(result, "include-hidden", options.includeHidden.toString());
    83	      if (options.level != null)
    84	        addAttr(result, "level", options.level.toString());
    85	      if (options.name != null) {
    86	        String name = escapeForAttributeSelector(options.name, options.exact != null && options.exact);
    87	        addAttr(result, "name", name);
    88	      }
    89	      if (options.pressed != null)
    90	        addAttr(result, "pressed", options.pressed.toString());
    91	    }
    92	    return result.toString();
    93	  }
    94	
    95	  private static String escapeRegexForSelector(Pattern re) {
    96	    // Even number of backslashes followed by the quote -> insert a backslash.
    97	    return toJsRegExp(re).replaceAll("(^|[^\\\\])(\\\\\\\\)*([\"'`])", "$1$2\\\\$3").replaceAll(">>", "\\\\>\\\\>");
    98	  }
    99	
   100	  static String escapeForTextSelector(Object value, boolean exact) {
   101	    if (value instanceof Pattern) {
   102	      return escapeRegexForSelector((Pattern) value);
   103	    }
   104	    if (value instanceof String) {
   105	      return gson().toJson(value) + (exact ? "s" : "i");
   106	    }
   107	    throw new IllegalArgumentException("text parameter must be Pattern or String: " + value);
   108	  }
   109	
   110	  private static String escapeForAttributeSelector(Object value, boolean exact) {
   111	    if (value instanceof Pattern) {
   112	      return escapeRegexForSelector((Pattern) value);
   113	    }
   114	    if (value instanceof String) {
   115	      // TODO: this should actually be
   116	      //   cssEscape(value).replace(/\\ /g, ' ')
   117	      // However, our attribute selectors do not conform to CSS parsing spec,
   118	      // so we escape them differently.
   119	      return '"' + ((String) value).replaceAll("\\\\", "\\\\\\\\").replaceAll("\"", "\\\\\"") + '"' + (exact ? "" : "i");
   120	    }
   121	    throw new IllegalArgumentException("Attribute can be String or Pattern, found: " + value);
   122	  }
   123	
   124	  private static String toJsRegExp(Pattern pattern) {
   125	    return "/" + pattern.pattern() + "/" + toJsRegexFlags(pattern);
   126	  }
   127	}

    51	  FrameImpl(ChannelOwner parent, String type, String guid, JsonObject initializer) {
    52	    super(parent, type, guid, initializer);
    53	
    54	    name = initializer.get("name").getAsString();
    55	    url = initializer.get("url").getAsString();
    56	    if (initializer.has("parentFrame")) {
    57	      parentFrame = connection.getExistingObject(initializer.getAsJsonObject("parentFrame").get("guid").getAsString());
    58	      parentFrame.childFrames.add(this);
    59	    }
    60	    for (JsonElement item : initializer.get("loadStates").getAsJsonArray()) {
    61	      loadStates.add(loadStateFromProtocol(item.getAsString()));
    62	    }
    63	  }
    64	
    65	  private static WaitUntilState loadStateFromProtocol(String value) {
    66	    switch (value) {
    67	      case "load": return LOAD;
    68	      case "domcontentloaded": return DOMCONTENTLOADED;
    69	      case "networkidle": return NETWORKIDLE;
    70	      case "commit": return COMMIT;
    71	      default: throw new PlaywrightException("Unexpected value: " + value);
    72	    }
    73	  }
    74	
    75	  @Override
    76	  public ElementHandle querySelector(String selector, QuerySelectorOptions options) {
    77	    if (options == null) {
    78	      options = new QuerySelectorOptions();
    79	    }
    80	    JsonObject params = gson().toJsonTree(options).getAsJsonObject();
    81	    params.addProperty("selector", selector);
    82	    JsonElement json = sendMessage("querySelector", params, NO_TIMEOUT);
    83	    JsonObject element = json.getAsJsonObject().getAsJsonObject("element");
    84	    if (element == null) {
    85	      return null;
    86	    }
    87	    return connection.getExistingObject(element.get("guid").getAsString());
    88	  }
